     324             :    (b) set a breakpoint on main() and on alloc_intercept()

     326             :    (d) when the breakpoint on main() is hit, set trace_alloc_ptr to A
     327             :            (e.g., "p trace_alloc_ptr=0x123456" in gdb)
     328             :    (e) continue execution: the breakpoint on alloc_intercept() will be hit
     329             :        when the suspect node is created
     330             : 
     331             : Note that this may not work as expected for addresses determined after the IL
     332             : has been read from a file, because the nodes were allocated at a different
     333             : address before the IL was written out.
     334             : 
     335             : Note that this variable is not re-initialized if the front end is called
     336             : multiple times.
     337             : 
     338             : On many modern operating systems, repeated runs of the same binary may not
     339             : yield the same addresses.  In that case, in a configuration with
     340             : MAINTAIN_ALLOCATION_SEQUENCE_NUMBER set to TRUE, the technique above can be
     341             : used instead by setting the variable trace_seq_number to the entry to be

    6168         320 : void compute_il_prefix_size(void)
    6169             : /*
    6170             : Compute the size of the IL entry prefix for file scope IL entries in this
    6171             : translation unit.  On the initial call, also compute the prefix size
    6172             : for non-file-scope entities.
    6173             : */

    6175         320 :   int   aligned_size;
    6176             : 
    6177             :   /* All entries allocated in the file scope have a prefix.  If we are
    6178             :      doing orphan processing, they also have an orphan pointer.  In
    6179             :      secondary translation units they also have a translation unit
    6180             :      copy address pointer. */
    6181         320 :   file_scope_entry_prefix_size =
    6182         320 :             (is_primary_translation_unit ? 0
    6183             :                                 : SPACE_FOR_TRANS_UNIT_COPY_ADDRESS_POINTER) +
    6184             : #if ORPHAN_PROCESSING_NEEDED
    6185             :             SPACE_FOR_FS_ORPHAN_POINTER +

    6187             :             SPACE_FOR_IL_ENTRY_PREFIX;
    6188             :   /* Compute the additional space required so that the prefix is a multiple
    6189             :      of the host alignment that is required. */
    6190         320 :   aligned_size = file_scope_entry_prefix_size;
    6191         320 :   do_host_alignment(aligned_size);
    6192         320 :   file_scope_entry_prefix_alignment_offset = aligned_size - 
    6193             :                                              file_scope_entry_prefix_size;
    6194             :   /* Set the prefix size to the aligned size. */
    6195         320 :   file_scope_entry_prefix_size = aligned_size;
    6196             :   /* Compute the size of the non-file-scope entry prefix and the associated
    6197             :      alignment offset. */
    6198         320 :   if (is_primary_translation_unit) {
    6199         320 :     non_file_scope_entry_prefix_size = SPACE_FOR_IL_ENTRY_PREFIX;
    6200         320 :     do_host_alignment(non_file_scope_entry_prefix_size);
    6201         320 :     non_file_scope_entry_prefix_alignment_offset =
    6202             :                   non_file_scope_entry_prefix_size - SPACE_FOR_IL_ENTRY_PREFIX;
    6203             :   }  /* if */
    6204         320 : }  /* compute_il_prefix_size */
